 6476 // The registrar notes several more specific domains available in each state,
 6477 // such as state.*.us, dst.*.us, etc., but resolution of these is somewhat
 6478 // haphazard; in some states these domains resolve as addresses, while in others
 6479 // only subdomains are available, or even nothing at all. We include the

 6481 // entities.
